name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Guestroom (Double Bed) (Terrace)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:Advantages:
1) Yan Zi at the front desk handled the check-in procedures, explained the hot spring breakfast and other matters very clearly, and her voice was very gentle. The service was very good!
2) Parking is convenient, both on the ground and underground.
3) The room is large and the big bed is very comfortable. The hotel facilities are quite complete, including fitness, swimming pool, Starbucks, and Haagen-Dazs.
4) The hotel is directly connected to the Jiletang Hot Spring Hall, with mixed bathing areas and separate areas for men and women. We only experienced the mixed bathing area, which had a strong smell of disinfectant water, and did not experience other areas.
Disadvantages:
1) The hotel has not started the air conditioning in May, and there is only fresh air in the room, which needs to be cooled by opening windows and electric fans. It was raining heavily outside when we checked in, and the room felt damp with the window open. This is a bit stingy.
2) There is a problem with the room door card system. If the gesture is wrong and the card is not swiped successfully the first time, there will be no response when swiping again. You need to wait for a few minutes for it to restart itself before swiping again. It is a waste of time and troublesome, and the staff themselves have encountered this problem.
3) The quality of the hotel breakfast is just so-so. You can tell that they are trying to reduce costs in the details, and the quality is obviously reduced. The hot milk is made with milk powder, the sausage tastes not very good, and the boiled corn is glutinous corn instead of sweet corn.

Overall, the room rate for May Day is a bit high, but there is nothing you can do about it during the peak holiday. The price-performance ratio is better on weekdays, and the platform discount room voucher is half cheaper than our May Day price on weekdays.
